ṣṭatvādivyapadeśaḥ pradhānasya saṃbhavati tathāpi na draṣṭṛtvādivyapadeśa saṃbhavati pradhānasyācetanatvena tairabhyupagamāt adṛṣṭo draṣṭāśrutaḥ śrotāmato mantāvijñāto vijñātā iti hi vākyaśeṣa iha tarhi akṣarātparataḥ paraḥ iti vyapadiśyata iti uttarasūtre tadvakṣyāma api cātra dve vidye veditavye ukte parā caivāparā ca iti tatrāparāmṛgvedādilakṣaṇāṃ vidyāmuktvā bravīti atha parā yayā darśitam viruddhaṃ tu tattejosṛjata ityanena śrutyantareṇa na ekavākyatvātsarvaśrutīnām bhavatvekavākyatvamaviruddhānām iha tu virodha uktasakṛcchrutasya sraṣṭuḥ sraṣṭavyadvayasaṃbandhāsaṃbhavāhūyośca prathamajatvāsaṃbhavādvikalpāsaṃbhavācceti naiṣa doṣaḥ teja sargasya taittirīyake tṛtīyatvaśravaṇāt tasmādvā etasmādātmana ākāśa saṃbhūtaḥ ākāśādvāyuḥ vāyoragniḥ iti aśakyā hīyaṃ śrutiranyathā pariṇetum śakyā tu pariṇetuṃ chāndogyaśrutiḥ tadākāśaṃ vāyuṃ ca sṛṣṭvā tattejosṛjata sū dvitīyodhyāyaḥ itina hīyaṃ śrutistejojanipradhānā satī śrutyantaraprasiddhāmākāśasyotpattiṃ vārayituṃ śaknoti ekasya vākyasya vyāpārayāsaṃbhavāt sraṣṭā tvekopi krameṇānekaṃ sraṣṭavyaṃ sṛjet  ityekavākyatvakalpanāyāṃ saṃbhavantyāṃ na viruddhārthatvena śrutitivyāna cāsmābhiḥ sakṛcchrutasya sraṣṭuḥ sraṣṭavyadvayasaṃbandhobhipreyate śrutyantaravaśena sraṣṭavyāntaropasaṃprahān yathā ca sarvaṃ khalvidaṃ brahma tajjalān ityatra sākṣādeva sarvasya vastujātasya brahmajatvaṃ śrūyamāṇaṃ na pradeśāntaravihitaṃ tejapramukhamutpattikramaṃ vārayati evaṃ tejasopi brahmajatvaṃ śrūyamāṇaṃ na śrutyantaravihitaṃ nabhaḥ pramukhamutpattikramaṃ vārayitumarhati nanu śamavidhānārthametadvākyam tajjalāniti śānta upāsīta iti śruteḥ naitatsṛṣṭivākyamtasmādetanna pradeśāntaraprasiddhaṃ kramamanuroddhumarhatītitattejosṛjata ityetatsṛṣṭivākyamatasmādatra yathāśruti kramo grahītavya iti netyucyatena hi tejaprāthamyānurodhena śrutyantaraprasiddho viyatpadārthaḥ parityaktavyo bhavati padārthadharmatvātkramasya api ca tattejosṛjata iti nātra kramasya vācakaḥ kaścicchabdosti arthāttu kramo gamyate sa ca vāyoragniḥ ityanena śrutyantaraprasiddhena krameṇa nivāryatevikasūtrabhāṣye lpasamuccayau tu viyattejaso prathamajatvaviṣayāvasaṃbhavānabhyupagamābhyāṃ nivāritautasmānnāsti śrutyorvipratiṣedhaḥ api ca chāndogye yenāśrutaṃ śrutaṃ bhavati ityetāṃ pratijñāṃ vākyopakrame śrutāṃ samarthayitumasamāmnātamapi viyat utpattāvupasaṃkhyātavyam kimaṅga punastaittirīyake samāmnātaṃ nabho na saṃgṛhyate yaccoktamaākāśasya sarveṇānanyadeśakālatvādbrahmaṇā tatkāryeśca saha viditameva tadbhavatiato na pratijñā hīyatena ca ekamevādvitīyam iti śrutikopo bhavati kṣīrodakavadbrahmanabhasoravyatirekopapatteriti atrocyatena kṣīrodakanyāyeneda meka vijñānena sarvavijñānaṃ netavyamamṛdādidṛṣṭāntapraṇayanāddhi prakṛtivikāranyāyenaivedaṃ sarvavijñānaṃ netavyamiti gamyatekṣīrodakanyāyena ca sarvavijñānaṃ kalpyamānaṃ na samyagvijñānaṃ syāt na hi kṣīrajñānagṛhītasyodakasya samyagvijñānagṛhītatvamastina ca vedasya puruṣāṇāmiva māyālīkavañcanādibhirarthāvadhāraṇamupapadyatesāvadhāraṇā ceyam ekamevādvitīyam iti śruti kṣīrodakanyāyena nīyamānā pīḍyeta na ca svakāryāpekṣayedaṃ vastvekadeśaviṣayaṃ sarvavijñānamevādvitīyatāvadhāraṇaṃ ceti nyāyyam mṛdādiṣvapi hi tatsaṃbhavāt na tadapūrvavadupanyapā sū dvitīyodhyāyaḥ sitavyaṃ bhavatiśvetaketo yannu somyedaṃ mahāmanā anūcānamānī stabdhosyuta tamādeśamaprākṣya yenāśrutaṃ śrutaṃ bhavati ityādinā tasmādaśeṣavastuviṣayamevedaṃ sarvavijñānaṃ sarvasya brahmakāryatāpekṣayopanyasyata iti draṣṭavyam yatpunaretaduktam asaṃbhavāgauṇī gaganayotpattiśrutiriti atra brūma GONGINES MANI yāvadvikāraṃ tu vibhāgo lokavat tuśabdosaṃbhavāśaṅkāvyāvṛttyartha na khalvākāśotpattāvasaṃbhavāśaṅkā kartavyāyato yāvatkiṃcidvikārajātaṃ dṛśyate ghaṭaghaṭikodaścanādi vā kaṭakakeyūrakuṇḍalādi vā sūcīnārācanistriṃśādi vā tāvāneva vibhāgo loke lakṣyatena tvavikṛtaṃ kiṃcitkutaścidvibhaktamupalabhyatevibhāgaścākāśasya pṛthivyādibhyovagamyate tasmātsopi vikāro bhavitumarhati etena dikkālamanaparamāṇvādīnāṃ kāryatvaṃ vyākhyātam nanvātmāpyākāśādibhyo vibhakta iti tasyāpi kāryatvaṃ ghaṭādivatprāpnotina ātmana ākāśa saṃbhūta iti śruteḥ yadi hyātmāpi vikāra syāt tasmātparamanyanna śrutamityākāśādi sarve kārye nirā sūtrabhāṣye pā tmakamātmanaḥ kāryatve sthāttathā ca śūnyavādaḥ prasajyetaātmatvāñcātmano nirākaraṇaśaṅkānupapattiḥ na hyātmāgantuka kasyacit svayaṃsiddhatvātna hyātmā ātmana pramāṇama pekṣya sidhyatitasya hi pratyakṣādīni pramāṇānyasiddhaprameyasiddhaye upādīyante na hyākāśādayaḥ padārthā pramāṇanirapekṣā svayaṃ siddhāḥ kenacidabhyupagamyanteātmā tu pramāṇādivyavahārāśrayatvātprāgeva pramāṇādivyavahārātsidhyatina cedṛśasya nirākaraṇaṃ saṃbhavatiāgantukaṃ hi vastu nirākriyate na svarūpam ya eva hi nirākartā tadeva tasya svarūpam na hyagnerauṣṇyamagninā nirākriyatetathā ahamevedānīṃ jānāmi vartamānaṃ vastu ahamevātītamatītataraṃ cājñāsiṣam ahamevānāgatamanāgatataraṃ ca jñāsyāmi ityatītānāgatavartamānabhāvenānyathābhavatyapi jñātavye na jñāturanyathābhāvosti sarvadā vartamānasvabhāvatvāttathā bhasmībhavatyapi dehe nātmana ucchedaḥvartamānasvabhāvādanyasvabhāvatvaṃ vā na saṃbhāvayituṃ śakyamevamapratyākhyeyasvabhāvatvādakāryatvamātmānaḥ kāryatvaṃ ca ākāśasya yattūktaṃ samānajātīyamakaṃ kāraṇadravyaṃ vyomro nāstīti tatpratyucyate na tāvatsamānajātīyamevārabhate na bhiBamsū dvitīyodhyāyaḥ najātīyamiti niyamostina hi tantūnāṃ tatsaṃyogānāṃ ca samānajātīyatvamasti dravyaguṇatvābhyupagamātna ca nimittakāraṇānāmapi turīvemādīnāṃ samānajātīyatvaniyamosti syādetat samavāyikāraṇaviṣaya eva samānajātīyatvābhyupagamaḥ na kāraṇāntaraviṣaya ititadapyanaikāntikam sūtragovārhyanekajātīyairekā rajjuḥ sṛjyamānā dṛśyatetathā sūtrairūrṇādibhiśca vicitrānkambalānvitanvatesattvadravyatvādyapekṣayā vā samānajātīyatve kalpyamāne niyamānarthakyam sarvasya sarveṇa samānajātīyakatvāt nāpyanekamevārabhate naikam iti niyamostiaṇumanasorādyakamarambhābhyupagamāt ekaiko hi paramāṇurmanaścādyaṃ karmārabhate na dravyāntaraiḥ saṃhatya ityabhyupagamyate dravyārambha evānekārambhakatvaniyama iti cet napariṇāmābhyupagamāt bhavedeṣa niyama yadi saṃyogasacivaṃ dravyaṃ dravyāntarasyārambhakamabhyupagamyetatadeva tu dravyaṃ viśeṣavadavasthāntaramāpadyamānaṃ kārya nāmābhyupagamyatetacca kvacidanekaṃ pariṇamate mṛdvījādi aṅkurādibhāvenakvacidekaṃ pariṇamate kṣīrādi dadhyādibhāvenaneśvaraśāsanamasti anekameva kāraṇaṃ kārya janayatīti ataḥ śrutiprāmāṇyādekasmādbrahmaṇa pā ākāśādimahābhūtotpattikrameṇa jagajjātamiti niścīyatetathā coktam upasaṃhāradarśanānneti cenna kṣīravaddhi iti sūtrabhāṣye yañcoktam ākāśasyotpattau na pūrvottarakālayorviśeṣa saṃbhāvayituṃ śakyata iti tadayuktam yenaiva viśeṣeṇa pṛthivyādibhyo vyatiricyamānaṃ nabha svarūpavadidānīmadhyavasīyate sa eva viśeṣa prāgutpatternāsīditi gamyateyathā ca brahma na sthūlādibhiḥ pṛthivyādisvabhāvaiḥ svabhāvavat asthūlamanaṇu ityādiśrutibhyaḥ evamākāśasvabhāvenāpi na svabhāvavadanākāśamiti śruteravagamyatetasmātprāgutpatteranākāśamiti sthitam yadapyuktaṃ pṛthivyādivaidharmyādā kāśasyājatvamiti tadpyasat śrutivirodhe satyutpattyasaṃbhavānumānasyābhāsatvopapatte utpattyanumānasya ca darśitatvātanityamākāśam anityaguṇāśrayatvāt ghaṭādivadityādiprayogasaṃbhavācca ātmanyanaikāntikamiti cet natasyaupaniṣadaṃ pratyanityaguṇāśrayatvāsiddheḥvibhutvādīnāṃ ca ākāśasyotpattivādinaṃ pratyasiddhatvāt yaccoktametat śabdācceti tatrāmṛtatvaśrutistāvādvayati amṛtā divaukasaḥ itivadraṣṭavyāutpattipralayayorupapāditatvāt ākāśavatsarvagatañca nitya ityapi prasiddhamahattvenākāśopamānaṃ kriyate niratiśayamahasū dvitīyodhyāyaḥ ttvāya na ākāśasamatvāya yathā iṣuriva savitā dhāvati iti kṣipragatitvāyocyate na iṣutulyagatitvāya tadvat etenānantatvopamānaśrutirvyākhyātājyāyānākāśāt ityādiśrutibhyaśca brahmaṇaḥ sakāśādākāśasyonaparimāṇatvasiddhi na tasya pratimāsti iti ca brahmaṇonupamānatvaṃ darśayati  atonyadārtam iti ca brahmaṇonyeṣāmākāśādīnāmārtatvaṃ darśayati tapasi brahmaśabdavadākāśasya janmaśrutegauṇatvamityetadākāśasaṃbhavaśrutyanumānābhyāṃ parihṛtam tasmākārya viyaditi siddham etena mātariśvā vyākhyātaḥ atideśoyam etena viyavyākhyānena mātariśvāpi viyadāśrayo vāyurvyākhyātaḥ tatrāpyete yathāyogaṃ pakṣā mātariśvāracayitavyāḥ  na vāyurutpadyate chandogādhikaraṇam nāmutpattiprakaraṇenāmnānādityeka pakṣaḥ asti tu taittirīyāṇāmutpattiprakaraṇe āmnānam ākāśādvāyu iti pakṣāntaram tataśca śrutyorvipratiṣedhe sati gauṇī vāyorutpattiśrutiḥ asaṃbhavāt ityaparobhiprāya asaṃbhavaśva saiṣānastamitā devatā yadvāyuḥ ityastamayapratiṣedhādamṛtatvādiśravaṇācca pratijñānuparodhādyāvadvikāraṃ ca visūtrabhāṣye pā bhāgābhyupagamādutpadyate vāyuriti siddhāntaḥ astamayapratiṣedhoparavidyāviṣaya āpekṣikaḥ agnyādīnāmiva vāyorasta mayābhāvāt kṛtapratividhānaṃ ca amṛtatvādiśravaṇam nanu vāyorākāśasya ca tulyayorutpattiprakaraṇe śravaṇāśravaṇayorekamevādhikaraṇamubhayaviṣayamastu kimatideśenāsati viśeṣa iti ucyate satyamevametat tathāpi mandadhiyāṃ śabdamātrakṛtāśaṅkānivṛttyarthoyamatideśaḥ kriyate saṃvargavidyādiṣu hyupāsthatayā vāyormahābhāgatvaśravaṇāt astamayapratiṣedhādibhyaśca bhavati nityatvāśaṅkā kasyaciditi asaṃbhavastu satonupapatteḥ viyatpavanayorasaṃbhāvyamānajanmanorapyutpattimupaśrutya brahmaṇopi bhavetkutaścidutpattiriti syātkasyacinmatitathā asaṃbhavādhivikārebhya evākāśādibhya uttareṣāṃ vikākaraṇam rāṇāmutpattimupaśrutya ākāśasyāpi vikārādeva brahmaṇa utpattiriti kaścinmanyetatāmāśaṅkāmapanetumidaṃ sūtram asaṃbhavastviti na khalu brahmaṇa sadātmakasya kutaścidanyataḥ saṃbhava utpattirāśaṅkitavyākasmāt  anupapatte sanmātraṃ hi brahma na tasya sanmātrādevotpatti nirātmakatvāt kathamasataḥ sajjāyeta iti ca ākṣepaśravaṇāt sa kāraṇaṃ karaṇādhipādhipo na cāsya kaścijjanitā na cādhipaḥ iti ca brahmaṇo janayitāraṃ vārayati viyatpavanayo punarutpatti pradarśitā na tu brahmaṇa sā astīti vaiṣamyam na ca vikārebhyo vikārāntarotpattidarśanādbrahmaṇopi vikāratvaṃ bhavitumarhati mūlaprakṛtyanabhyupagamenavasthāprasaṅgāt yā mūlaprakṛtirabhyupagamyate tadeva ca no brahmetyavirodhaḥ tejotastathā chāndogye sanmūlatvaṃ tejasa śrāvitam taittirīyake tu vāyumūlatvam tatra tejoyoniṃ prati śrutivipratipattau satyām tejodhi prāptaṃ tāvadbrahmayonikaṃ teja iti kuta  karaṇam sadeva ityupakramya tattejosṛjata ityupadeśāt sarvavijñānapratijñāyāśca brahmaprabhavatve sarvasya saṃbhavāt tajalān iti ca aviśeṣaśruteḥetasmājjāyate prāṇa iti ca upakramya śrutyantare sarvasyāviśeṣeṇa brahmajatvopadeśāttaittirīyake ca sa tapastaptvā idaṃ sarva sūtrabhāṣye pā masṛjata yadidaṃ kiṃca ityaviśeṣaśravaṇāttasmāt vāyoragni iti kramopadeśo draṣṭavyaḥ vāyoranantaramagniḥ saṃbhūta iti evaṃ prāpte ucyate teja ata mātariśvanaḥ jāyata iti kasmāt  tathā hyāhavāyoragniḥ iti avyavahite tejaso brahmajatve sati asati vāyujatve vāyoragniḥ itīyaṃ śrutiḥ kadarśitā syāt nanu kramārthaiṣā bhaviṣyatītyuktam neti brūmaḥ tasmādvā etasmādātmana ākāśa saṃbhūta iti purastāt saṃbhavatyapādānasya ātmanaḥ pañcamīnirdeśāt tasyaiva ca saṃbhavaterihādhikārāt parastādapi tadadhikāre pṛthivyā oṣadhayaḥ ityapādānapañcamīdarśanāt vāyoragniḥ ityapādānapañcamyevaiṣeti gamyateapi ca vāyorūrdhvamagniḥ saṃbhūtaḥ iti kalpya upapadārtha yogaḥ klaptastu kārakāryayoga vāyoragniḥ saṃbhūtaḥ ititasmādeṣā śrutirvāyuyonitvaṃ tejasovagamayati nanvitarāpi śrutirbrahmayonitvaṃ tejasovagamayati tattejosṛjata itina tasyāḥ pāraṃparyajatvepyavirodhātyadāpi hyāṃkāśaṃ vāyuṃ ca sṛṣṭvā vāyubhāvāpannaṃ brahma tejosṛjateti kalpyate tadāpi brahmajatvaṃ tejaso na virudhyate sū dvitīyodhyāyaḥ yathā tasyāḥ śṛtam tasyā dadhi tasyā āmikṣetyādi darśayati ca brahmaṇo vikārātmanāvasthānamtadātmāna svayamakuruta iti tathā ca īśvarasmaraṇaṃ bhavati  buddhirjñānamasaṃmoha ityādyanukramya bhavanti bhāvā bhūtānāṃ matta eva pṛthagvidhāḥ iti yadyapi buddhayādayaḥ svakāraṇebhyaḥ pratyakṣaṃ bhavanto dṛśyante tathāpi sarvasya bhāvajātasya sākṣātpraṇāḍyā vā īśvaravaṃśyatvāt etenākramasṛṣṭivādinyaḥ śrutayo vyākhyātāḥ tāsāṃ sarvathopapatteḥ kramavatsṛṣṭivādinīnāṃ tvanyathānupapatteḥ pratijñāpi sadūṃśyatvamātramapekṣate na avyavahitajanyatvam ityāvirodhaḥ āpaḥ atastathā hyāha ityanuvartateāpaḥ ata tejasaḥ jāyante kasmāt  tathā hyāha tadaposṛjata iti agne abadhirāpa iti ca sati vacane nāsti saṃ śaya tejasastu sṛṣṭi vyākhyāya pṛthivyā vyākhyāsyan apontariyāmiti āpa iti sūtrayāṃbabhūva karaṇam pṛthivyadhikārarūpaśavdāntarebhyaḥ tā āpa aikṣanta bahutha syāma prajāyemahīti tā annasūtrabhāṣye pā kārādhimasṛjanta iti śrūyatetatra saṃśaya kimanenānnaśabdena pṛthivyadhibrīhiyavādyabhyavahārya vā odanādyucyate kiṃ vā pṛthivītitatra prāptaṃ tāvat  vrīhiyavādi odanādi vā parigrahītavyamiti tatra hyannaśabdaḥ prasiddho lokevākyaśeṣopyetamarthamupoilayati tasmādyatra kacana varṣati tadeva bhūyiṣṭhamannaṃ bhavati iti vrīhiyavādyeva hi mati varṣaṇe bahu bhavati na pṛthi vīti karaṇam evaṃ prāpte brūmaḥ pṛthivyeveyamannaśabdenādbhayo jāyamānā vivakṣyata iti kasmāta  adhikārāt rūpāt śabdāntarācca adhikārastāvattattejosṛjata tadaposṛjata iti mahābhūtaviṣayo vartatetatra kramaprāptāṃ pṛthivīṃ mahābhūtaṃ vilamaya nākasmādbrīhyādiparigraho nyāyya tathā rūpamapi vākyaśeṣe pṛthivyanuguṇaṃ dṛśyateyatkṛṣṇaṃ tadnasya iti na hyodanāderabhyavahāryasya kṛṣṇatvaniyamosti nāpi brīhyādīnām nanu pṛthivyā api naiva kṛṣṇatvaniyamosti payapāṇḍurasyāṅgārarohitasya ca kṣetrasya darśanātnāyaṃ doṣa bāhulyāpekṣatvāt bhūyiṣṭhaṃ hi pṛthivyāḥ kṛṣṇaṃ rūpam na tathā śvetarohitepaurāṇikā api pṛthivīchāyāṃ sū dvitīyodhyāyaḥ śarvarīmupadiśanti sā ca kṛṣṇābhāsā ityata kṛṣṇaṃ B rūpaṃ pṛthivyā iti liṣyate śrutyantaramapi samānādhikāram adbhavaḥ pṛthivī iti bhavati tadyadpāṃ śara āsīttatsamahanyata sā pṛthivyabhavat iti capṛthivyāstu śrīhyāderutpattiṃ darśayati pṛthivyā oṣadhaya oṣadhībhyonnam iti ca evamadhikārādiṣu pṛthivyāḥ pratipādakeṣu satsu kuto brīhyādipratipatti asaṃbhavāt iti vyākhyātam pratijñāhānyā ca tatra siddhāntobhihita iha tu siddhāntasūtratvāt gauṇyā janmaśruterasaṃbhavāt iti vyākhyātamtadanurodhena tu ihāpi gauṇī janmaśrutiḥ asaṃbhavāt iti vyācakṣāṇaiḥ dvitīyodhyāyaḥ sū pratijñāhānirūpekṣitā syāt tatprākteśca itañca ākāśādīnāmiva prāṇānāmapi mukhyaiva janmaśruti yat jāyate ityekaṃ janmavācipadaṃ prāṇeṣu prākaśrutaṃ sat uttareṣvākāśādiṣvanuvartate etasmājjāyate prāṇa ityatra ākāśādiṣu mukhyaṃ janmeti pratiṣṭhāpitam tatsāmānyātprāṇeṣvapi mukhyameva janma bhavitumarhatina hi ekasminprakaraṇe ekasmiṃca vākye ekaḥ śabdaḥ sakṛduccarito bahubhiḥ saṃbadhyamāna kacinmukhya kvacidrauṇa ityadhyavasātuṃ śakyam vairūṇyaprasaṅgāt tathā sa prāṇamasṛjata prāṇācchraddhām ityatrāpi prāṇeṣu śrutaḥ sṛjatiḥ pareṣvapyu tpattimatsu śraddhādiṣvanuṣajyate yatrāpi paścācchūta utpattivacana śabdaḥ pūrvaiḥ saṃbadhyate tatrāpyeṣa eva nyāya yathā sarvāṇi bhūtāni vyuccaranti ityayamante paṭhito vyuccarantiśabda pūrvairapi prāṇādibhiḥ puruṣavacaso bhavanti itinirūpaṇaṃ ca pratipattya prativacanam parjanyapṛthivīpuruṣayoṣidhikaraṇam tsu pañcasvaniṣu śraddhāsomavṛṣṭayannaretorūpāḥ pañca āhutīrdarśayitvā iti tu pañcamyāmāhutāvāpa puruṣavacaso bhavanti bhavanti ititasmādadbhiḥ pariveṣṭito jīvo raṃhati vrajatīti gamyate nanvanyā śrutiḥ jalūkāvatpūrvadehaṃ na muñcati yāvanna dehāntaramākramatīti darśayatitṛṇajalāyukā ititatrāpyappariveṣṭitasyaiva karmopasthāpitapratipattavyadehaviṣayabhāvanādīrghībhāvamātraṃ jalūkayopamīyata ityavirodha evaṃ śrutyukte dehāntarapratipattiprakāre sati yā puruṣamatiprabhavā kalpanā vyāpināṃ karaṇānāmātmanaśca dehāntarapratipattau karmavaśāttilābhastatra bhavati kevalasyaivātmano vṛttilābhastatra bha vati indriyāṇi tu dehavadabhinavānyeva tatra tatra bhogasthāne utpadyante mana eva vā kevalaṃ bhogasthānamabhipratiṣṭhate jīva eva vā utplutya dehāddehāntaraṃ pratipadyate śuka iva vṛkṣāvṛkṣāntaram ityevamādyāḥ tāḥ sarvā eva anādartavyāḥ śrutivirodhāt sūtrabhāṣye pā nanu udāhṛtābhyāṃ praśnaprativacanābhyāṃ kevalābhiradbhiḥ saṃpariṣvakto raṃhatīti prāpnoti apaśabdaśravaṇasāmarthyāt tatra kathaṃ sāmānyena pratijñāyate sarvaireva bhūtasūkṣmaiḥ saṃpariṣvakto raṃhatīti  ata uttaraṃ paṭhati tryātmakatvāttu bhūyastvāt tuśabdena coditāmāśaṅkāmucchinatti tryātmikā hi āpaḥ trivṛtkaraṇaśruteḥtāsvārambhikāsvabhyupagatāsvitaradapi bhūtadvayamavaśyamabhyupagantavyaṃ bhavati tryātmakaśca dehaḥ trayāṇāmapi tejobannānāṃ tasminkāryopalabdheḥ punaśca tryātmakaḥ tridhātutvāt tribhirvātapittaśleṣmabhiḥna sa bhūtāntarāṇi pratyākhyāya kevalābhiradbhirārabdhuṃ śakyate tasmādbhūyastvāpekṣoyamāpa puruṣavacasa iti praśnaprativacanayorapśabdaḥ na kaivalyāpekṣa sarvadeheṣu hi rasalohitādidravabhūyastvaṃ dṛśyate nanu pārthivo dhāturbhūyiṣṭho deheṣūpalakṣyatenaiṣa doṣaitarāpekṣayā apāṃ bāhulyaṃ bhaviṣyati dṛśyate ca śukraśoṇitalakṣaṇepi dehabīje dravabāhulyam karma ca nimittakāraṇaṃ dehāntarārambhekarmāṇi ca agnihotrādīni somājyapayaḥprabhṛtidravadravyavyapāśrayāṇi karmasamavāyinyaśca āpaḥ śraddhāśabdoditāḥ saha karmabhirgulokākhyennau hūyanta itisū tṛtīyodhyāyaḥ vakṣyatitasmādapyapāṃ bāhulyaprasiddhiḥ bāhulyācca apaśabdena sarveṣāmeva dehabījānāṃ bhūtasūkṣmāṇāmupādānamiti niravadyam prāṇagateśca prāṇānāṃ ca dehāntarapratipattau gatiḥ śrāvyatetamutkrāmantaṃ prāṇonutkrāmati prāṇamanūtkrāmantaṃ sarve prāṇā anūtkāmanti ityādiśrutibhiḥsā ca prāṇānāṃ gatirnāśrayamantareṇa saṃbhavatītyataḥ prāṇagatiprayuktā tadāśrayabhūtānāmapāmapi bhūtāntaropasṛṣṭānāṃ gatirarthādvagamyatena hi nirāśrayā prāṇā kacidgacchanti tiṣṭhanti vā jīvato darśanāt agnyādigatiśruteriti cenna bhāktatvāt syādetat  naiva prāṇā dehāntarapratipattau saha jīvena gacchanti agnyādigatiśruteḥ tathā hi śruti maraṇakāle vāgādaya prāṇā agnyādīndevāngacchantīti darśayatiyatrāsya puruṣasya mṛtasyāgniṃ vāgadhyeti vātaṃ prāṇaḥ ityādinā iti cet na bhāktatvātvāgādīnāmagnyādigatiśrutirgauṇī lomasu keśeṣu ca adarśanātoṣadhīrlomāni vanaspatīnke sūtrabhāṣye pā śā iti hi tavāmnāyate na hi lomāni keśācotluya oṣadhīrvanaspatīṃca gacchantīti saṃbhavatina ca jīvasya prāṇopādhipratyākhyāne gamanamavakalpate nāpi prāṇairvinā dehāntare upabhoga upapadyatevispaṣṭaṃ ca prāṇānāṃ saha jīvena gamanamanyatra śrāvitamaato vāgādyadhiṣṭhātrīṇāmagnyādidevatānāṃ vāgādyupakāriṇīnāṃ maraṇakāle upakāranivṛttimātramapekṣya vāgādayognyādīngacchantītyupacaryate prathameśravaṇāditi cenna tā eva hyupapatteḥ syādetat kathaṃ puna pañcamyāmāhutāvāpaḥ puruṣavacaso bhavanti ityetat nirdhārayituṃ pāryate yāvatā naiva prathamegnāvapāṃ śravaṇamasti  iha hi lokaprabhṛtayaḥ pañcāgnayaḥ pañcānāmāhutīnāmādhāratvenādhītā teṣāṃ ca pramukhe asau vāva loko gautamāgni ityupanyasya tasminne tasminnannau devā śraddhāṃ juhvati iti śraddhā homyadravyatvena āveditāna tatra āpo homyadravyatayā śrutā yadi nāma parjanyādiṣūttareṣu caturdhvagnidhvapāṃ homyadravyatā parikalpyeta parikalpyatāṃ nāma teṣu hotavyatayopāttānāṃ somādīnāmabahulatvopapatteprathame tvau śrutāṃ śraddhāṃ parityajya aśrutā āpaḥ parikalpyanta itisū tṛtīyodhyāyaḥ sāhasametat śraddhā ca nāma pratyayaviśeṣaḥ prasiddhisāmarthyāttasmādayuktaḥ pañcamyāmāhutāvapāṃ puruṣabhāva iti cet naiṣa doṣaḥ hi yataḥ tatrāpi prathamegnau tā evāpaḥ śraddhāśabdenābhipreyante kuta  upapatte evaṃ hyādimadhyāvasānasaṃgānāt anākulametadekavākyamupapadyateitarathā punaḥ pañcamyāmāhutau apāṃ puruṣavacastvaprakāre pṛṣṭe prativacanāvasare prathamāhutisthāne yadyanapo homyadravyaṃ śraddhāṃ nāmāvatārayet tataḥ anyathā praśnonyathā prativacanamityekavākyatā na syāt  iti tu pañcamyāmāhutāvāpa puruṣava caso bhavanti iti ca upasaṃharan etadeva darśayati śraddhākārya ca somavṛṣṭayādi sthūlībhavadabbahulaṃ lakṣyatesā ca śraddhāyā aptve yukti kāraṇānurūpaṃ hi kārya bhavati na ca śraddhākhya pratyayaḥ manaso jīvasya vā dharma san dharmiṇo niṣkṛṣya homāyopādātuṃ śakyate paśvādibhya iva hṛdayādīni iti āpa eva śraddhāśabdā bhaveyuḥ śraddhāśabdaścāpsūpapadyate vaidikaprayogadarśanāt śraddhā vā āpa iti tanutvaṃ śraddhāsārūpyaṃ gacchanti āpo dehabījabhūtā ityataḥ śraddhāśabdāḥ syuyathā siṃhaparākramo naraḥ siṃhaśabdo bhavati śraddhāpūrvakakarmasamavāyāca apsu śraddhāśabda upapadyate ma caśabda sūtrabhāṣye pā iva puruṣeṣuśraddhā hetutvācca śraddhāśabdopapattiḥ āpo hāsmai śraddhāṃ saṃnamante puṇyāya karmaṇe iti śruteḥ aśrutatvāditi cenneṣṭādikāriṇāṃ pratīteḥ pondo athāpi syāt  praśnaprativacanābhyāṃ nāma āpa śraddhādikrameṇa pañcamyāmāhutau puruṣākāraṃ pratipadyeranna tu tatsaṃpariṣvaktā jīvā raheyuḥ aśrutatvāt na hyatra apāmiva jīvānāṃ śrāvayitā kaścicchabdostitasmāt raṃhati saṃpariṣvaktaḥ ityayuktam iti cet naiṣa doṣaḥ kuta  iṣṭādikāriṇāṃ pratīte atha ya ime grāma iṣṭāpūrte dattamityupāsate te dhūmamabhisaṃbhavanti ityupakramya iṣṭādikāriṇāṃ dhūmādinā pitṛyāṇena pathā candraprāptiṃ kathayati ākāśācandramasameṣa somo rājā iti ta evehāpi pratīyante tasminnetasminnannau devā śraddhāṃ juhvati takhā āhuteḥ somo rājā saṃbhavati iti śrutisāmānyāt teṣāṃ ca agnihotradarśapūrṇamāsādikarmasādhanabhūtā dadhipayaḥprabhṛtayo dravadravyabhūyastvātpratyakṣameva āpaḥ santi tā āhavanīye hutā sūkṣmā āhutyopūrvarūpā satya tāniṣṭādikāriṇa āśrayanti teṣāṃ ca śarīraṃ naidhanena vidhānenāntyegnāvṛtvijo juhvati sū tṛtīyodhyāyaḥ  asau svargāya lokāya svāhā ititatastā śraddhāpūrvaka karmasamavāyinya āhutimayya āpopūrvarūpā satyaḥ tāniṭādikāriṇo jīvānpariveṣṭya amuṃ lokaṃ phaladānāya nayantī ti yat tadatra juhotinā abhidhīyate śraddhāṃ juhvatīti tathā ca agnihotre ṣaṭpranīnirvacanarūpeṇa vākyaśeṣeṇa te vā ete āhutī hute utkrāmata ityevamādinā agnihotrāhutyoḥ phalārambhāya lokāntaraprāptidarśitā tasmādāhutīmayībhiradbhiḥ saṃpariṣvaktā jīvā rahanti svakarmaphalopabhogāyeti te kathaṃ punaridamiṣṭādikāriṇāṃ svakarmaphalopabhogāya raṃhaṇaṃ pratijñāyate yāvatā teṣāṃ dhūmapratīkena vartsanā candramasamadhirūḍhānāmannabhāvaṃ darśayatieṣa somo rājā taddevānāmantraṃ taṃ tevā bhakṣayanti iti te candraṃ prāpyānnaṃ bhavanti tāṃstatra devā yathā somaṃ rājānamāpyāyasvāpakṣīya svetyevametāṃstatra bhadhyanti iti ca samānaviṣayaṃ śrutyantaram  na ca vyāghrādibhiriva devairbhakṣyamāṇānāmupabhoga saṃbhavatīti ata uttaraṃ paṭhati bhāktaṃ vānātmavittvāttathāhi darśayati  sūtrabhāṣye pā go na syāt vā śabdaśvoditadoṣavyāvartanārtha bhāktameṣāmannatvam na mukhyammukhye hyannatve svargakāmo yajeta ityevaṃjātīyakādhikāraśrutiruparudhyetacandramaṇḍale cediṣṭādikāriṇāmupabhokimarthamadhikāriṇa iṣṭādi āyāsabahulaṃ karma kuryuḥ annaśabdaśvopabhoga hetutvasāmānyāt anannepyupacaryamāṇo dṛśyate yathāviśonaṃ rājñāṃ paśavonnaṃ viśāmiti tasmādiṣṭastrīputramitrabhṛtyādibhiriva guṇabhāvopagatairiṣṭādikāribhiryatsukhaviharaṇaṃ devānām tadevaiṣāṃ bhakṣaṇamabhipretam na modakādivaccarvaṇaṃ nigaraṇaṃ vā na ha vai devā ananti na pibantyetadevāmṛtaṃ dṛṣṭvā tṛpyanti iti ca devānāṃ carvaṇādivyāpāraṃ vārayati teṣāṃ ca iṣṭādikāriṇāṃ devānprati guṇabhāvopagatānāmapyupabhoga upapadyate rājopajīvināmitra parijanānām anātmavittvācca iṣṭādikāriṇāṃ devopabhogyabhāva upapadyatetathā hi śrutiranātmavidāṃ devopabhogyatāṃ darśayati  atha yonyāṃ devatāmupāstenyosāvanyohamasmīti na sa veda yathā paśurevaṃ sa devānām itisa cāsminnapi loke iṣṭādibhiḥ karmabhi prīṇayanpaśuvaddevānāmupakaroti amuṣminnapi loke tadupajīvī tadādiṣṭaṃ phalamupabhuñjānaḥ paśuvadeva devānāmupakarotīti gamyate sū tṛtīyodhyāyaḥ anātmavittvāt tathā hi darśayati ityasya aparā vyākhyā anātmavido hyete kevalakarmiṇa iṣṭādikāriṇaḥ na jñānakarmasamuccayānuṣṭhāyinaḥ pañcāgnividyāmiha ātmavidyetyupacaranti prakaraṇātpañcāgnividyāvihīnatvāñcemiṣṭādikāriṇāṃ guṇavādenānnatvamudbhāvyate pañcāgnivijñānapraśaṃsāyaipañcāgnivigreha vidhitsitā vākyatātparyāvagamāttathā hi śrutyantaraṃ candramaṇḍale bhogasadbhāvaṃ darśayati sa somaloke vibhūtimanubhūya punarāvartate iti tathā anyadapi śrutyantaram atha ye śataṃ pitṝṇāṃ jitalokānāmānandāḥ sa ekaḥ karmadevānāmānando ye karmaṇā devatvamabhisaṃpadyante iti iṣṭādikāriṇāṃ devai saha saṃvasatāṃ bhogaprāptiṃ darśayati evaṃ bhāktatvādannabhāvavacanasya iṣṭādikāriṇotra jīvā raṃhantīti pratīyate tasmāt raṃhati saṃpariṣvaktaḥ iti yuktamevoktam kṛtātyayenuśayavāndṛṣṭasmṛtibhyāṃ yathetamanevaṃ ca iṣṭādikāriṇāṃ dhūmādinā vartmanā candramaṇḍalamadhirūḍhānāṃ bhuktabhogānāṃ tataḥ pratyavaroha āmnāyate tasminyāvatsaṃsūtrabhāṣye pā pātamuṣitvāthaitamevādhvānaṃ punarnivartante yathetam ityārabhya kṛtātyayā yāvat ramaṇīyacaraṇā brāhmaṇādiyonidhikaraṇam māpadyante kapūyacaraṇā śvādiyonimiti tadaṃ vicārya ki niranuśayā bhuktakṛtsnakarmāṇovarohanti āhosvitsānuśayā iti kiṃ tāvatprāptam  niranuśayā itikuta  yāvatsaṃpātam iti viśeṣaṇātsaṃpātaśabdenāta karmāśaya ucyate saṃpatanti anena asmā llokāta amuṃ lokaṃ phalopabhogāyeti yāvatsaṃpātamuṣitvā iti ca kṛtsnasya tasya kṛtasya tatraiva bhuktatāṃ darśayati teṣāṃ yadā tatparyavaiti iti ca śrutyantareṇaiṣa evārtha pradairyate syādetat yāvadamuṣmilloke upabhoktavyaṃ karma tāvadupabhuta iti kalpayiṣyāmītinaivaṃ kalpayituṃ śakyate yatkiṃca ityanyatra parāmarśātprāpyāntaṃ karmaṇastasya yatkiceh karotyayam tasmāllokātpunaraityasmai lokāya karmaṇe iti hi aparā śruti yatkica ityaviśeṣaparāmarśena kṛtsnasyeha kṛtasya karmaṇaḥ tatra kṣayitatāṃ darśayati api ca prāyaṇamanārabdhaphalasya karmaṇobhivyañjakam prākprāyaṇāt ārabdhaphalena karmaṇā pratibaddhasyābhivyaktyanupapatte tacca aviśeṣādyā vatkiṃcidanārabdhaṃphalaṃ tasya sarvasyābhivyañjakam sū tṛtīyodhyāyaḥ na hi sādhāraṇe nimitte naimittikamasādhāraṇaṃ bhavitumarhati na hyaviśiṣṭe pradīpasaṃnidhau ghaṭobhivyajyate na paṭa ityupapadyate tasmānniranuśayā avarohantītyevaṃ prāpte AGRA brūmaḥ kṛtātyayenuśayavāniti yena karmabṛndena candramasamārūḍhāḥ phalopabhogāya tasminnupabhogena kṣayite teṣāṃ yadammayaṃ śarīraṃ candramasyupabhogāyārabdham tat upabhogakṣayadarśanaśokāgnisaṃparkātpravilīyate savitṛkiraṇasaṃparkādiva himakarakāḥ hutabhugarci saṃparkādiva ca ghṛtakāṭhinyam tata kṛtātyaye kṛtasyeṣṭādeḥ karmaṇa phalopabhogenopakṣaye sati sānuśayā evemamavarohantikena hetunā  dṛṣṭasmṛtibhyāmityāha tathā hi pratyakṣā śruti sānuśayānāmavarohaṃ darśayati tadya iha ramaṇīyacaraṇā abhyāśo ha yatte ramaṇīyāṃ yonimāpadyeranbrāhmaṇayoniṃ vā kṣatriyayoniṃ vā vaiśyayoniṃ vātha ya iha kapūyacaraṇā abhyāśo ha yatte kapūyāṃ yonimāpadyerañśvayoniṃ vā sūkarayoniṃ vā cāṇḍālayoniṃ vā iti caraṇaśabdenānuśaya sūcyata iti varṇayiṣyati dṛṣṭaścāyaṃ janmanaiva pratiprāṇyuccāvacarūpa upabhoga pravibhajyamāna ākasmikatvāsaṃbhavādanuśayasadbhāvaṃ sūcayati abhyudayapratyavāyayo sukṛtaduṣkṛtahetutvasya sāmānyataḥ śāstreṇāvagamitatvāt smṛtiha sūtrabhāṣye pā rapi varṇā āśramāśca svakarmaniṣṭhā pretya karmaphalamanubhūya tata śeṣeṇa viśiṣṭadeśajātikularūpāyuḥ śrutavṛtta vittasukhamedhaso janma pratipadyante iti sānuśayānā mevāvarohaṃ darśayati kaḥ punaranuśayo nāmetikecittāvadāhuḥ svargārthasya karmaṇo bhuktaphalakhāvaśeṣaḥ kaścidanuśayo nāma bhāṇḍānusārisnehavat yathā hi snehabhāṇḍaṃ ricyamānaṃ na sarvātmanā ricyate bhāṇḍānusāryeva kaścitsnehaśeṣovatiṣṭhate tathā anuśayopīti nanu kāryavirodhitvāddṛṣṭasya na bhuktaphalasyāvaśeṣāvasthānaṃ nyāyyam nāyaṃ doṣa na hi sarvātmanā bhuktaphalatvaṃ karmaṇa pratijānīmahe nanu niravaśeṣakarmaphalopabhogāya candramaṇḍalamārūḍhābāḍham tathāpi svalpakarmāvaśeṣamātreṇa tatrāvasthānaṃ na labhyateyathā kila kaścitsevaka sakalai sevopakaraṇai rājakulamupasṛptaśvirapravāsātparikṣīṇabahūpakaraṇachatrapādukādimātnāvaśeṣo na rājakulevasthātuṃ śaknoti evamanuśayamātraparigraho na candramaṇḍalevasthātuṃ śaknotīti tumbe na caitadyuktamiva na hi svargārthasya karmaṇo bhuktaphalasyāvaśeṣānuvṛttirupapadyate kāryavirodhitvāt ityuktam nanvetadapyuktamna svargaphalasya karmaṇo nikhilasya bhuktaphalatvaṃ bhaviṣyatīti tadetadpeśalam svargārthaṃ kila karma svargastha antyhsū tṛtīyodhyāyaḥ syaiva svargaphalaṃ nikhilaṃ na janayati svargacyutasyāpi kaṃcitphalaleśaṃ janayatītina śabdapramāṇakānāmīdṛśī kalpanā avakalpatesnehabhāṇḍe tu snehaleśānuvṛttirdṛṣṭatvādupapadyatetathā sevakasyopakaraṇaleśānuvṛttiśca dṛśyatena vih tathā svargaphalasya karmaṇo leśānuvṛttirdṛśyatenāpi kalpayituṃ śakyate svargaphalatvaśāstravirodhāt avaśyaṃ caitadevaṃ vijñeyam na svargaphalasyeṣṭāde karmaṇo bhāṇḍānusārisnehavadekadeśonuvartamānonuśaya iti yadi hi yena sukṛtena karmaṇā iṣṭādinā svargamanvabhūvan tasyaiva kaścidekadeśonuśayaḥ kalpyeta tato ramaṇīya evaikonuśaya syāt na ākāśādiṣu pravarṣaṇānteṣu na kiṃcitkarmavyāpāraṃ parāmṛśati evaṃ brīhyādijanmanyapi tasmānnāstyatra sukhaduḥkhabhāktvamanuśayinām yatra tu sukhaduḥkhabhāktvamabhipraiti parāmṛśati tatra karmavyāpāram ramaṇīyacaraṇā kapūyacaraṇā iti api ca mukhyenuśayināṃ brīhyādijanmani brīhyādiṣu lūyamāneṣu kaṇḍyamāneṣu pacyamāneṣu bhakṣyamāṇeṣu ca tadbhimāninonuśayinaḥ pravaseyuḥyo hi jīvo yaccharīramabhimanyate sa tasminpīḍyamāne pravasati iti prasiddham tatra brīhyādibhāvādretaḥsigbhāvonuśayināṃ nābhilapyetasaṃsargamātramanuśayināṃmanyādhiṣṭhiteṣu vrīhyādiṣu bhavati etena ataḥsūtrabhāṣye janermukhyārthatvaṃ pratibrūyāt upabhogasthānatvaṃ ca sthāvarabhāvasyana ca vayamupabhogasthānatvaṃ sthāvarabhāvasyāvajānīmahebhavatvanyeṣāṃ jantūnāmapuṇyasāmarthyena sthāvarabhāvamupagatānām etat upabhogasthānam candramasastu avarohantonuśayino na sthāvarabhāvamupabhuñjata ityācakṣmahe piā aśuddhamiti cenna śabdāt yatpunaruktampaśuhiṃsādiyogādaśuddhamādhvarikaṃ karma tasyāniṣṭamapi phalamavakalpata ityato mukhyamevānuśayināṃ trīhyādijanma astutatra gauṇī kalpanā anathiṃketitatparihriyate na śāstra hetutvāddharmādharmavijñānasyaayaṃ dharmaḥ ayamadharma iti śāstrameva vijñāne kāraṇam atīndriyatvāttayo aniyatadeśakālanimittatvācca yasmindeśe kāle nimitte ca yo dharmonuṣṭhīyate sa eva deśakālanimittāntareṣvadharmo bhavati tena na śāstrādṛte dharmādharmaviṣayaṃ vijñānaṃ kasyacidasti śāstrācca hiṃsānugrahādyātmako jyotiṣṭomo dharma ityavadhārita sa kathamaśuddha iti śakyate vaktum nanu na hiṃsyātsarvā bhūtāni iti śāstrameva bhūtaviṣayāṃ hiṃsām adharma ityavagamayatibāḍham utsargastu saapavādoyaṃ ca agnīṣomīyaṃ paśumālabheta iti utsargāsū tṛtīyodhyāyaḥ pavādayocaṃ vyavasthitaviṣayatvam tasmādviśuddhaṃ karma vaidina śiṣṭairanuṣṭhīyamānatvāt anindyamānatvāccatena na tasya kam pratirūpaṃ phalam jātisthāvaratvam na ca śvādijanmavadapi vrīhyādijanma bhavitumarhatitaddhi kapūyacaraṇānadhikṛtya ucyatenaivamiha vaiśeṣikaḥ kaścidhikārosti ataścandrasthalaskhalitānāmanuśāyināṃ brīhyādisaṃśleṣamātraṃ tadbhāva ityu pacaryate retaḥ sigyogotha itaśca vrīhyādisaṃśleṣamātraṃ tadbhāvaḥ yatkāraṇaṃ vrīhyādibhāvasyānantaramanuśayināṃ retaḥ sigbhāva āmnāyateyo yo hyanamatti yo reta siñcati tadbhūya eva bhavati iti na cātra mukhyo reta sigbhāva saṃbhavaticirajāto hi prāptayauvano reta sigbhavatikathamiva anupacaritaṃ tadbhāvam adyamānānānugatonuśayī pratipadyate  tatra tāvadavaśyaṃ reta sigyoga eva reta sigbhāvobhyupagantavyaḥtadvat trīhyādibhāvopi vrīhyādiyoga evetyavirodhaḥ yone śarīram atha reta sigbhāvasthānantaraṃ yonau niṣikte retasi yoneradhi śarīram anuśayinām anuśayaphalopabhogāya jāyatasūtrabhāṣye prā ityāha śāstram tadya iha ramaṇīyacaraṇā ityāditasmā dapya vagamyatenāvarohe brīhyādibhāvāvasare taccharīrameva sukhaduḥkhānvitaṃ bhavatīti tasmāt BHASHYA Volume NOWAYbrahmasūtrabhāṣyam tṛtīyo bhāgaḥśrīḥ viṣayānukramaṇikā tṛtīyodhyāyaḥ dvitīyaḥ pādaḥ tattvaṃ padārthavivekaḥ  saṃdhyādhikaraṇam saṃgatipradarśanapūrvakam uddeśyaṃ tvaṃ padārtha vivecayitum atha rathān iti śrutimavaṣṭabhya tathyarūpāṃ svapnasṛṣṭimudāhṛtya mithyāpratyayā sarvepi samyañca iti pratijānānāṃ pūrvavādināṃ pakṣasya udbhāvanam ya eṣa supteṣu ityādikāṭhakaśrutimavalambya prājñakartṛkatvaṃ hetukṛtya svapnasṛṣṭe pāramārthikatvasādhanam vyāpaka viruddhopanyāsena vastutvaṃ vyāvartya māyāmātratvasiddhāntaḥ pṛṣṭham śubhāśubhaphalānvayavyatirekābhyāṃ śāstreṇa ca vi rodhasya parihāra svayaṃ jyotiṣṭavivecanānuguṇaṃ rathādyabhāvavacanameva śrutyā vyākhyeyam sthādisṛṣṭivacanaṃ tu bhaktyā iti vivicya paroktanirasanam prājñakartṛkatvasya parābhimatahetoḥ asiddhibādhābhyāmābhāsīkaraṇam paramātmāṃśasya jīvasya satyasaṃkalpasya sāṃkalpikī svapne sthādisṛṣṭiiti śaṅkāyāḥ jīvasya jñānaiśvaryatirodhānamupapādya parihāra tadbhāvādhikaraṇama suṣuptiparīkṣārthī viṣayopanyāsaḥ nāḍīpurītatparamātmanāṃ suṣutasthānatayā śrayamāṇānām ekārthānāṃ vikalpe brahmabhāvāniyamāt karmaṇaivāpavarga saṃbhāvayatāṃ pūrvavādināṃ matasya udbhāvanam samuccayena nāḍyādīni svāpāya upasarpatīti siddhāntaḥ ekavi bhaktinirdeśasya anaikāntikatvapradarśanam sāpekṣaśrutyanurodhena nirapekṣaśrutiṃ nītvā samuccayabādhanirasanam jīvasyādheyatvamabhyupagataṃ parityajya brahmātmatvameva jīvasya suṣute brahmādhāratvam tadupādhika raṇamātrādhāratayā tu jīvasya suṣusārambhāya nāḍīpurītadādhāratvam iti atulyārthatānirū paṇena vikalpavighaṭanam asatyapavāde jīvasyautsargikaṃ brahmatādātmyaṃ na suṣupte anyathayituṃ śakyamiti vikalpāyoge yuktyantaram paramātmātirikteṣu sthāneṣu viśeṣavijñānasyāvaśya katayā suteranupapattiḥ guṇapradhānabhāvena samuccayaḥ na samapradhānatayeti niṣkarṣa ātmanaḥ prabodhāpādānatāṃ svāpādhikāre śiṣyamāṇāmupanyamya siddhāntaṃdṛḍhīkaraṇam karmānusmṛtiśabda vidhyadhikaraṇam jalabindunyāyena supta evaṃ pratibudhyata iti na niyantuṃ śakyateiti pūrvapakṣa karmaśeṣānuṣṭhānadarśanam anusmṛtiṃ śrutiṃ karmavidyā vidhyanupapatti copanyasya suptasyaiva punarutthānamiti niyamasya samarthanam utsūtraṃ siddhāntayuktiviśeṣāṇāmupanyāsaḥ vivekahetoḥ karmaṇovidyāyāśca sadbhāvāt jīvasya brahmābhedāca jalabindunyāyasya vighaṭanam  mugdhādhikaraṇama prasiddhāvasthānāṃ mūrchā anyatameti pūrvapakṣaḥ dehadhāraṇābhāvāt viṣayamātrānupalabdheśca mugdhasya jāgrato vailakṣaṇyasamarthanam niḥsaṃjñakatvāt prāṇoṣmaṇorbhāvācca svapnamṛtibhyāṃ mūrchāyā bhedasya pratipādanam suṣuptamohayo prayojanakāraṇalakṣaṇabhedebhyo bhedasya samarthanam ardhena suṣuptapakṣasya bhavati mugdhatvam ardhena avasthāntarapakṣasya iti siddhāntaḥ ubhayaliṅgādhikaraṇam tatpadārthanirūpaṇārambhe pratijñā bhinnākārayogo brahmaṇaḥ śāstrīya iti śaṅkāyābhedasya upāsanārthatvāt abhede tātparyāt neti nirasanam tatpradhānatvaṃ vinigamakamāśritya anākārabrahmāvadhāraṇam prakāśadṛṣṭāntena aupādhikamākārayogamanākāreubhayaliṅga śrutyupanyāsena saṃśayabījodghāṭanam svata upādhito vā parasya brahmaṇaḥ ubhayaliṅgatvānupapatternirviśeṣameva pratipattavyam iti siddhānta pyupāsanārtha samarthya ākāravadviṣayāṇāmapi śrutīnāṃ gatipradarśanam nirviśeṣatvānukūlatayā anyāpoha mugvena brahma darśayantīnāṃ śrutismṛtīnām upanyāsaḥ jalasūryakādiśāstrīyadṛṣṭāntasya prakṛtānukūlatayā ekaniyogapratīteḥ brahmopāsanāvākyānā mekavākyatetyabhimānasya acodanātantratvādbrahmavijñānaṃ prapañca pravilayaṃ ca aśakyatvāt anupapatteḥ anyathāsiddhatvācca niyogagocarādapanīya śithi līkaraṇam upanyāsaḥ uktadṛṣṭāntavaiṣamyaśaṅkā tatpratividhānaṃ ca anupraveśaśrutyupanyāsena uktadṛṣṭāntadṛḍhīkaraṇam niṣprapañcatvaparatayā sanmātratvaparatayā ca adhikaraṇadvayaṃ kalpayatāṃ svayūthyānāṃ matasyodbhāvanam evamadhikaraṇāntarārambhasya sarvathā vaiyarthyamiti tannirasanam ākāra śrutīnāmapi taditarākārapravilayo gatiriti matamanūdya brahmopāsanāvākyānāṃ pārthagarthyasamarthanena tannirasanam prapañcapakṣe ucchedāt brahmapakṣa aniyojyatvāt jīvasya niyojyatāvighaṭanena niyogavārtāyā vārtīkaraṇam niyogābhyupagamepi sādhyānubandhabhedādekaniyogatvamasiddhamiti nigamanam prakṛtaitāvattvādhikaraṇam neti netīti pratiṣedhe saṃśayamupanyasya brahmāpi brahmaiva vā pratiṣedhyam iti pakṣayoḥ sahetukamupanyāsaḥ na hyanāśrayaḥ pratiṣedhaḥ śakyaḥ pratipattum na ca brahmapare śabde brahmaṇi pramāṇe sati tatpratiṣedhopi pramāṇavān nāpi vedāntā brahma pratiṣedhāyaiva mahatā prayatnena pratipādayanti iti tayoḥ pakṣayornirasanam prakṛtaitāvatvaṃ hi pratiṣedhatīti sūtrāvayavavibhajanam mūrtāmūrtaviṣayatayā bhūtarāśivāsanārāśiviṣayatayā kṛtsnaviṣayapratiṣedhaparyavasāyivīṃ sārūpatayā ca pratiṣedhadvayasya nayanam na hyetasmāditi netyanyatparamasti iti vākyaṃ etasmādityasya ādiṣṭādeśanaparāmarśitayā vākyabhedena vākyaikyena ca dvidhā yojayitvā tadanurodhena tato bravīti ca bhūyaḥ ityasya anyatparamastītyetadviṣayatayā atha nāmadheyamityetadviṣayatayā ca vibhajanam abhāvo na brahmābhāve kramate ayogyatvādityatra śrutismṛtibhyāṃ hetoḥ sādhanam śrutismṛtibhyāṃ brahmaṇaḥ saṃrādhanagrāhyatāpradarśanam saṃrādhyasaṃrādhakabhāve jīvaprājñayorahikuṇḍalavat pra kāśāśrayavacca bhedābhedayorbhāvikayorevāvirodhaṃ matāntaraṃ nirasya cidātmana aupādhikabhedabhānepi svata ekarasatvameveti advaitaniṣkarṣeṇa nigamanam parādhikaraṇama phalādhikaraṇam setūnmānasaṃbandhabhedavyapadeśānāṃ vyākhyānapuraḥsaraṃ brahmaṇonyattatvamastīti pūrvapakṣasyodbhāvanam setuvyapadeśasya vidhārakatvasāmānyaparatayā parihāraḥ unmānavyapadeśasya ādhyānārthatayā parihāra saṃbandhabhedavyapadeśayoraupādhikatayā parihāra anyapratiṣedhasamāśrayaṇa eva sarvaṃgatatvamanyātmanaḥ prāmāṇikamupapadyate iti upasaṃhāraḥ upapatteḥ śruteśca īśvara eva phalaheturiti siddhāntenopakramaḥ karmaṇo vā sūkṣmā kāciduttarāvasthā phalasya vā pūrvāvasthā apūrva nāma kalpyamānaṃ vidhiviṣayasya yāgasya phalotpādakatvamupapādayatīti jaimini matasyodbhāvanam apūrvāgrahaṃ vihāya īśvaraprasādonurudhyatām karmāpekṣādapūrvāpekṣādvā īśvarāt phalamiti suviśadaṃ bhavet iti bādarāyaṇaniṣkarṣaḥ tṛtīya pādaguṇopasaṃhāraḥ sarvavedāntapratyayādhikaraṇama nirupādhibrahmatattvagocaraṃ vijñānaṃ manvānasya bhedābhedacintāvatārākṣepaḥ sopādhikabrahmaprāṇādiviṣayāsu upāsanāsu bhedābhedavimarśa upapanna iti parihāra nāmarūpadharmaviśeṣapunaruktiprabhṛtīnāṃ bhedahetūnāmupalambhāt prativedāntaṃ vijñānabheda iti pūrvapakṣaḥ saṃyogarūpacodanākhyāviśeṣāt vijñānānāṃ sarvavedāntapratyayatvamiti siddhāntaḥ pañcābhividyāprāṇasaṃvādādiṣu utpattigata eva guṇabhedo vaiśvadevīvat kathaṃ na bhindyāt iti viśeṣāśaṅkāyāḥ parihāraḥ śirovratasya svādhyāyadharmatvopapādanena vidyābhedakatvavighaṭanam prāyadarśananyāyena upāsanānāmapi sarvavedāntapratyayatvasiddhiḥ ityupasaṃhāraḥ upasaṃhārādhikaraṇam sarvavedāntapratyayatve sarvavijñānānāṃ guṇopasaṃhāraḥ phalamiti nirṇaya vyāptyadhikaraṇama anyathātvādhikaraṇama vedyabhedanirūpaṇena vājināṃ chandogānāṃ ca udgīthavidyā arthavādasaṃjñāsāmyepi bhinnā iti niṣkarṣaḥ sarvābhedādhikaraṇama omityetadakṣaramityatra sāmānādhikaraṇye adhyāsāpavādakatvaviśeṣaṇapakṣāṇāṃ nirūpaṇam gauṇyā lakṣaṇāto durbalatvāt niṣphalatvāt padāntaravaiyarthyācca adhyāsāpavādakatvapakṣān nirasya viśeṣaṇapakṣeṇa siddhāntaḥ ānandādyadhikaraṇama prāṇasaṃvāde vasiṣṭhatvādiguṇānāmanuktānāmapi ekapradhānasaṃbaddhānāṃ koṣītakibrāhmaṇagatena evaṃśabdena parāmraṣṭuṃ yogyatvādupasaṃhāra iti nirṇa vāstavānāṃ vidheyānāṃ ca guṇānāṃ vastudharmatayā ca anuṣṭheyatayā ca avyavasthāvyavasthe vyavatiṣṭhete iti vivecanam ādhyānādhikaraṇam indriyebhyaḥ parā hyarthāḥ ityādikāṭhakaśrutau sarveṣāmeva arthādīnāṃ paratvaṃ pratipipādayiṣitamiti pūrvapakṣaḥ dṛṣṭaprayojanatvāt ādarātiśayācca puruṣaparatvaprati pādanārthoyaṃ saṃdarbha iti siddhāntaḥ ātmagṛhītyadhikaraṇam ātmāvā idameka eva ityāditaittirīyakaśrutau lokasṛṣṭivacanāt sūtrātmaivābhilapyate iti pūrvapakṣa ākāśapūrvikāyāṃ sṛṣṭau yathā kvacittejapūrvikāyāḥ sṛṣṭerabhidhānaṃ tathā mahābhūtasṛṣṭayanabhidhānena lokasṛṣṭayabhidhānaṃ na virudhyate paramātmagrahaṇa eva prāgutpatterātmaikatvāvadhāraṇamāñjasamavaṃkalpate iti paramātmaivābhilapyate iti siddhāntaḥ sadupakramasya chāndogyagatasya saṃdarbhasya ātmopakramasya ca vājasaneyakagatasya kimaikārthyam āhosvidarthabheda iti saṃśayopanyāsena kalpāntarārambhaḥ āmnānatantratvādarthaparigrahasya upakramatantratvādupasaṃhārasya arthabheda evocitaḥ tādātmyopadeśaśca saṃpattiparatayā neya iti pūrvapakṣaḥ sadeva  ekameva ityādyavadhāraṇaṃ tādātmyapratipādanāyāmevāvakalpate na tādātmyasaṃpādanāyām sāmānyopakramaśca na vākyaśeṣagatena viśegheṇa virudhyatesacchabdārthopi na mukhyādātmanonyaḥ saṃbhavati iti pratipādyābheda iti siddhāntaḥ kāryākhyānādhikaraṇam chandogānāṃ vājasaneyināṃ ca prāṇavidyāprakaraṇe yat aśiśiṣatām aśitavatāṃ ca ubhayata ācamanam anagnatācintanaṃ ca pratīyate tadubhayamapi vidhīyate apūrvatvāt vispaṣṭavidhivibhaktikatvādvā ācamanameva vidhīyate iti pakṣayorudbhāvanam A smārtasya ācamanasya vyāpakatvāt dṛṣṭisāhacaryā t samidho yajatītyādivat vartamānāpadeśasyāpi vidhikṣamatvāt jartilayavāgvā vā juhuam yāt ityādivat vidhivibhakterapi avivakṣitatvasaṃbhavācca vāsovijñānameva vidhīyate nācamanam iti siddhāntaḥ samānādhikaraṇama agnirahasyabṛhadāraṇyakayo śāṇḍilyavidyā a bhyāsādhikaraṇanyāyena bhinnati pūrvapakṣaḥ samānaguṇapunaḥśravaṇasya viprakṛṣṭavidyāpratyabhijñāpakatvenānyaparatvasaṃbhavādabhyāsādhikaraṇanyāyāpravṛtte vidyaikatvamiti siddhāntaḥ saṃbandhādhikaraṇam saṃbhṛtyadhikaraṇam bṛhadāraṇyake satyavidyāyāmādiśyamānayorupani do saṃkara iti svarūpamātraprādhānyābhiprāyeṇa pūrvapakṣaḥ saviśeṣaṇasyaiva pradhānatvāt atideśaliṅgācca tayovrvyavastheti siddhāntaḥ iti siddhāntaḥ saṃbhṛtyādīnāṃ guṇānāṃ śāṇḍilyādividyāsu ṣoḍaśakalādividyāsu ca pratyabhijñāsaṃbhavādupasaṃhāra iti pūrvapakṣaḥ asādhāraṇadharmāṇāmapratyabhijñānādanupasaṃhāra puruṣavidyādhikaraṇam vedhādyadhikaraṇama taittirīyakatāṇḍinoḥ puruṣavidyā puruṣayajñatvamaragāvabhṛthatvādisāmyādekaivaiti pūrvapakṣa bhūyovalakṣaṇyānna vidyekyamiti siddhāntaḥ hānyadhikaraṇam vidyāsaṃnidhipaṭhitānāṃ pravidhyādimantrāṇāṃ pravargyādikarmaṇāṃ ca anyatra viniyuktānāmapi saṃnighisāmarthyāt vidyārthatvenāpi pratipattiḥ bṛhaspatisavadṛṣṭāntena khādiratvādidṛṣṭāntena vā iti pūrvapakṣa prabalaiḥ śrutyādibhiranyatra viniyuktānām avirodhepi durbalasaṃnidhimātreṇa na saṃbhavati vi grāsu viniyogaḥ iti siddhāntaḥ yatra hānamātraṃ sukṛtaduṣkṛtayoḥ śrūyate tatra aśrūyamāṇaṃ
